  <div class="es reveal">En la oscuridad,<br>una sola luz.</div>

  <div class="en reveal">In the dark, a single light.</div>

</section>


<!-- ORIGIN TEXT -->


<section class="origin-text">

  <div class="eyebrow reveal">— Origen</div>

  <h2 class="reveal">Every coast has its keepers.<br>Ours keep a light.</h2>

  <p class="reveal">Casa Faro is named for the lighthouses of México's coast. A single light, kept for a stranger. The oldest hospitality we know.</p>

  <p class="reveal">The bottle takes their shape. The mark — an arched door — is the way in.</p>

</section>


<!-- BOTTLE -->


<section class="bottle">

  <div class="img" aria-label="Casa Faro bottle"></div>

  <div class="body">

    <div class="eyebrow">— El Frasco</div>

    <h3 class="reveal">Hand-thrown.<br>Fired twice. Unlabeled.</h3>

    <p>Stoneware ceramic, the clay of México's coast. Sealed in wax. The mark is pressed into the body before firing.</p>

    <p>No paper. No glass. What the bottle holds is meant to be poured slowly, and the bottle kept after.</p>

  </div>

</section>


<!-- LUZ + TASTING NOTES -->


<section class="luz">

  <div class="name reveal">LUZ</div>

  <div class="kind reveal">The first light</div>

  <p class="desc reveal">A blanco. Tahona-crushed. Unaged. <em>What the agave is, before anything is done to it.</em></p>

<script>

  // Nav color shift on scroll

  const nav = document.getElementById("nav");

  const hero = document.querySelector(".hero");

  const trigger = hero.offsetHeight - 80;

  window.addEventListener("scroll", () => {

    if (window.scrollY > trigger) nav.classList.add("scrolled");

    else nav.classList.remove("scrolled");

  }, { passive: true });


  // Reveal

  const io = new IntersectionObserver(entries => {

    entries.forEach(e => { if (e.isIntersecting) e.target.classList.add("in"); });

  }, { threshold: 0.2 });

  document.querySelectorAll(".reveal").forEach(el => io.observe(el));

</script>


</body>

</html>
